 The work of this unique bridge connecting Dibrugarh to Pasighat in Arunachal Pradesh will be completed by July this year
 railway ke adhikariyon ke mutabik bogibil pul ke naam se mashhoor pul ko july tak puraa kar diya jayega
 According to railway ministry officials, the bridge will be inaugurated by Prime Minister Narendra Modi
 bataa den, bogibil pul ko puraa karne ke liye raat din kaam kiya ja rahaa he
 All the pillars of the bridge have been installed here
 ab bas ek chota sa hissaa baaki he jisko kaaphi teji se puraa kiya ja rahaa he
 The Bogibeel Bridge is special in the sense that trains will run on it and cars and trucks will also be able to run on the highway built on it
 4
 The specialty of the 94 km long Bogibeel bridge is that it is built by welding
 is tarah kaa or itnaa lanbaa rail or road pul bharat main pehla he
 According to Mahendra Singh, Chief Engineer Construction of Bogibeel Bridge, 4 by July this year
 94 kilometre lambey is pul kaa nirmaan kaary puraa ho jayega
 There is a 3 line road above India's first and second longest railway and road bridge in Asia and below it is a dual rail line
 yah pul bramhaputra ke jal str se 32 meter kii oonchai par he
 The special thing is that such technology has made the bridge connecting Sweden and Denmark
 bogibil pul kii takanic kii shreshthata kaa andaja isi baat se lagaaya ja saktaa he ki isko banane main denmark se takanic lee gai to vahiin isaki testing kaa kaam germany ne kiya
 Director of the Ministry of Railways, Information and Publicity, Ved Prakashbogibil is very hopeful about the bridge, saying that this bridge will prove to be a symbol of development in the Northeast
 iske alaava is ilaake main awajahi kaa ek bada upyogi saadhan banegaa
 He said that the armed forces deployed along the Chinese border will also be well supported by Bogibeel
 railway adhikariyon ke mutabik train se dibrugarh se arunachal pradesh jane ke liye vyakti ko guwahati hokar janaa hota he
 And for this, he has to cover a distance of more than 600 kilometers
 is pul ke ban jane se yah yatra kaaphi aasaan ho jaaegi
 According to the 1985 Assam Accord, the Central Government agreed to build the Bogibeel Bridge over the Brahmaputra
 iske 11 saal baad bogibil pul ko 1996 main hi manjuuri mil gai thi
 But its construction started in 2002 by the government of Atal Bihari Vajpayee
 upie sarkaar ne 2007 main ise rashtriya pariyojna ghoshit kar diya tha
 The construction of India's longest and strategically important Bogibeel bridge connecting Assam's Dibrugarh to Pasighat in Arunachal had slowed down since 2002
 khaas baat yah he ki congress kii sarkaar ne 2009 main iskaa udghaatan karne kaa lakshya rakhaa tha, lekin yah ho na sakaa
 After the formation of Modi's government in 2014, work on the Bogibeel Bridge started rapidly and today it is in a state of completion
 bogibil pul dibrugarh shahar se 17 kilometre duuri par brahmaputra nadi par ban rahaa he
 The estimated cost of the Bogibeel bridge is 5800 crores
 is pul ke ban jane se brahmaputra ke dakshini kinare or uttari kinare par maujuud railway line aapas main jud jaaenge
 The Chalo Khowa and Moran hot railway stations on the southern side of the Brahmaputra have been completed
 vahiin duusari taraf rangiya se aane vaali railway line ko bogibil brij ke uttari hisse tak pahunchaa diya gaya he
 The station on the northern side of the Brahmaputra River is ready
 railway line bhi bich chuki he
 Tangani and Dhamal railway stations will be connected through the Bogibeel bridge
 brahmaputra nadi dibrugarh ilaake main kaaphi badi nadi he
 This river is so large that its width is measured up to kilometers here
 bogibil gaanv ke paas main brahmaputra nadi ko do tatbandhon se baandha gaya he
 The 10 km wide river is dammed and covered within 5 km
 nadi ko baandhakar is par lohe ke bade-bade tukade aapas main welding ke jariye jode gaye hai
 a large number of welding rods have been used to construct this bridge
 railway ke chif ejeeniyar construction mahendra singh ke mutabik pul ke nirmaan main takreeban 35 lakh bori cement kaa istemaal hua he
 The bridge is built on the lines of state-of-the-art Triangle Truss
 pul ko banane ke liye di ke aakaar main bade-bade khambhe daale gaye hai
 According to the railway engineer, 42 heavy pillars have been built for the bridge
 in khambhon ko brahmaputra nadi ke taale main wel foundation banaakar jamaaya gaya he
 Each pillar is inserted inside the Brahmaputra river to a depth of 65 meters
 is pul ko banane ke liye sabase behtareen cement kaa istemaal kiya gaya he
 According to the project's Chief Engineer, the Bogibeel Bridge has been strengthened considerably
 vajah yah he ki brahmaputra kaa yah ilaaka bukamp ke lihaaj se sabase khatarnaak jone main aata he
 Therefore, the bridge has been made capable of withstanding more than 8 magnitudes of earthquakes
 is pul ke khambhe itane zyada majboot banaae gaye hai, jisase brahmaputra kii badi se badi baadh kaa is par thodaa bhi asar na pade
 Bogibeel's bridge is strategically important for India
 bhartiya sena or surakshabalon ko arunachal or assam ke sabhi hisson ke liye ol time connactivity dene ke liye yah pul mahatvapurn bhoomika nibhaayega
 Through this, many places in Arunachal can be connected directly to the railway line
 bharat sarkaar ne pehle hi tawang ke liye railway line bichaane kaa elaan kar diya he
 In such a situation, the Bogibeel bridge will work to connect Arunachal completely to different stations of Indian Railways

 inputah IANS There are all kinds of misconceptions about the existence of Princess Jodha Bai
 unka ullekh aamtaur par mughal samraat akbar kii patni or jahangir kii maa ke rup main miltaa he, lekin jodhabai ke kaalpanik hone kii bhi khabaren aati rahi hai
 Now a new book claims Jodha Bai to be Portuguese
 itihaaskaaron ne jodhabai ko apane-apane nazariye se pesh kiya he
 Aishwarya Rai Bachchan has portrayed the life of Jodha Bai in the Bollywood film 'jodha-akbar'
 goa ke lekhak louis di asees koriya ne apni kitaab 'portuguese india and mughal relations 1510-1735' main kaha he ki jodhabai vastav main ek portugali mahila thim, jinka naam donna maaria masahrenhas tha, jo portugali jahaaj se arab sagar hote hue ain or jise 1500veen shatabdi ke madhya main gujarat ke sultan bahadur shah ne pakad kar samraat akbar ko bhent kar diya tha
 Donna was accompanied by her sister Juliana
 koriya ne panaji main kitaab ke locarpan kaarykram se itar se kaha, "jab donna maaria akbar ke darbar main pahunchin to akbar ko usase pyaar ho gaya
 At that time Akbar was 18 years old and Donna was 17 years old
 akbar pehle se shaadishuda tha, baavjood iske usne donna ke prati aasakt hokar use or uski choti bahan juliana ko apane haram main rakh liya
 " koriya kehete hai, "portugali or catholic yah sweekaar nahin kar paae ki unke samudaay kaa koi shaks haram main rahe, jabaki duusari taraf mughal yah sweekaar nahin kar sakate the ki firangi (isai) samudaay (jinhone shuru se hi mughalon ke viruddh hallaa bol rakhaa tha) kii mahila mughal kii patni bane
 Because of this, the British and the Mughal historians of that period created confusion about Jodhbai
 " He said that this is the reason why the documents of Akbar and Jehangir do not know the existence of Jodha Bai

 The 173-page book, published by Broadway Publishing House, states that Maria Mascarenhas may be Jahangir's mother, and she is often referred to as maryam-ul-zamani, and in ancient and popular legends she is called Jodhabai or Harkabai Also known as koriya ne kaha ki mariyam-ul-jamaani kaa mughal dastavejon main jahangir kii maa ke rup main kahin bhi zikr nahin he

 kya jahangir kaa janm mahaan rajput samrajya kii kisi beti se hua tha

 isi aupchaarikta ke chalate ab radimaid mandap kii maang bad gai he

 Once again, two gold smuggling gangs have been busted at the Mumbai airport
 air intelegence unit (eaiu) ne suraksha jaanch ke dauraan chaar aropiyon ke paas se 41 lakh rupee kaa sona baraamad kiya he
 An accused caught was smuggling gold by hiding the gold inside the speaker
 air intelegence unit ne buudhvaar or guuruuvaar ko mumbai airport parsone kii taskarikarne vaale do girohon par nakel kasi he
 During the search of the goods of Afzal, Salim and Wagle, who were returning to Mumbai from Bhubaneswar, security officials recovered illegal gold worth Rs 15 lakh from their belongings
 teenon aropiyon par maamla darj kar liya gaya
 In the second case, on Thursday, the AIU recovered gold worth Rs 26 lakhs while searching the belongings of a man named Mohammad Abdul Shukur returning to India from Kuwait

 The Tawa reservoir is located on the Tawa river in Hoshangabad district of Madhya Pradesh
 wildlife safari kaa lutf lene ke liye yah ekadam makul jagah he
 Madhya Pradesh provides cruise for this safari on the tourist department river
 yah satapura neshnal park kii pashchimi seemaa kaa bhi kaam karata he
 Madhya Pradesh Tourism Department has developed this reservoir as Tawa Resorts
 satapura ke jangalon main baagh, tendue, boar, chaar singon vaale hiran or bahut se anya jaanwaron kii prajatiyaan dekhne ko mil sakati hai
 Here you can also see a four-meter crocodile
 tawa jalaashya se suryaast dekhnaa yaadgaar anubhav rahata he
 Cruises usually enjoy this safari in three to four hours
 tawa kaise pahunchenhavaai margah kareebi airport bhopal (120 kimi)
 Rail route: The nearest major railway station is Hoshangabad (45 km) by road: 30 km from Tawa Resorts

 yah saal kaa vah vakt hota he jab aap vittiya yojanaayen banaate hai
 They can affect your financial future
 yahaan kuch nuskhe die ja rahe hai, jinase aap apni vittiya sthiti ko lambey vakt ke liye majboot kar sakate hai
 Every person who earns a tax plan has to pay tax
 so shuru main hi 80si ke niyam ke hisaab se nivesh karnaa shuru kar den
 Instead of looking at your financial advisor at the last moment, start the process early and make a complete plan for the amount invested to reduce the tax burden
 pipief jaise jariyon, jinamein nivesh par byaaj miltaa he, ko jitna jaldi ho, shuru kar den
 When it is an equity-related product like ELSS or a tax-saving joint fund, starting it early in the year means accumulating more units through SIP
 sahi beemaa chunebima (jivan, swasthya aadi) ko nivesh ke taur par na samajhen, balki use kisi anjaane khatre se bachaav ke saadhan ke rup main len
 Get out of the common belief that taking insurance only helps in saving tax
 beemaa ko jivan ke khatre se suraksha ke taur par len
 If you have taken an insurance plan, then see if the amount of insurance is sufficient to protect your family according to the current standard of living
 agar aisa nahin he to ek or beemaa yojana le len
 If you are only dependent on the health insurance scheme provided by the office, then you need to understand the full specifics and utility of that policy
 yah sunishchit karen ki aap par nirbhar parijanon ko is swasthya beemaa yojana kaa laabh mil rahaa he yaa nahin
